7,"blastmirna","Positions of miRNAs along the genome are shown. A BLASTN of genomic sequence regions against <a rel=""external"" href=""http://www.mirbase.org/"">miRBase</a> sequences is performed, and hits are clustered and filtered by E value. Aligned genomic sequence is then checked for possible secondary structure using RNAFold. If evidence is found that the genomic sequence could form a stable hairpin structure the locus is used to create a miRNA gene model. The resulting BLAST hit is used as supporting evidence for the miRNA gene. See <a href=""/info/genome/genebuild/ncrna.html"" class=""cp-external"">article</a>.","miRNAs (miRBase)",1,1,NULL,NULL,77795,"2018-10-19 15:24:57",NULL,0
